<T><V>|nel |mez|zo |del |cam|min |di |no|stra |vi|ta |</V>
<V>|mi |ri|tro|vai |per |u|na |sel|va o|scu|ra |</V>
<V>|ché |la |di|rit|ta |via |e|ra |smar|ri|ta |</V>
<T><V>|ahi |quan|to a |dir |qual |e|ra è |co|sa |du|ra |</V>
<V>|e|sta |sel|va |sel|vag|gia e |a|spra e |for|te |</V>
<V>|che |nel |pen|sier |ri|no|va |la |pa|u|ra |</V>
<T><V>|tan|t’ è |a|ma|ra |che |po|co è |più |mor|te |</V>
<V>|di|rò |de |l’ al|tre |co|se |ch’ i’ |v’ ho |scor|te |</V>
<V>|ma |poi |ch’ i’ |fui |al |piè |d’ un |col|le |giun|to |</V>

<V>|tal |mi |fe|c’ io |di |mia |vir|tu|de |stan|ca |</V>
<T><V>|e |tan|to |buo|no ar|di|re al |cor |mi |cor|se |</V>
<V>|ch’ i’ |co|min|ciai |co|me |per|so|na |fran|ca |</V>
<V>|oh |pie|to|sa |co|lei |che |mi |soc|cor|se |</V>
<T><V>|e |te |cor|te|se |ch’ u|bi|di|sti |to|sto |</V>
<V>|a |le |ve|re |pa|ro|le |che |ti |por|se |</V>
<V>|tu |m’ hai |con |di|si|de|rio il |cor |di|spo|sto |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ i’ |son |tor|na|to |nel |pri|mo |pro|po|sto |</V>
<V>|tu |du|ca |tu |se|gno|re e |tu |ma|e|stro |</V>
<V>|in|trai |per |lo |cam|mi|no al|to e |sil|ve|stro |</V>
<T><V>|per |me |si |va |ne |la |cit|tà |do|len|te |</V>
<V>|per |me |si |va |ne |l’ et|ter|no |do|lo|re |</V>
<V>|per |me |si |va |tra |la |per|du|ta |gen|te |</V>
<T><V>|giu|sti|zia |mos|se il |mio |al|to |fat|to|re |</V>
<V>|fe|ce|mi |la |di|vi|na |po|de|sta|te |</V>
<V>|la |som|ma |sa|pï|en|za e ’l |pri|mo a|mo|re |</V>
<T><V>|di|nan|zi a |me |non |fuor |co|se |cre|a|te |</V>

<V>|co|me |la |re|na |quan|do |tur|bo |spi|ra |</V>
<T><V>|e |io |ch’ a|vea |d’ er|ror |la |te|sta |cin|ta |</V>

<V>|e |che |gen|t’ è |che |par |nel |duol |sì |vin|ta |</V>

<T><V>|e |poi |ch’ a |ri|guar|dar |ol|tre |mi |die|di |</V>

<V>|per |ch’ io |dis|si |ma|e|stro or |mi |con|ce|di |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ i’ |sap|pia |qua|li |so|no e |qual |co|stu|me |</V>

<V>|com’ |i’ |di|scer|no |per |lo |fio|co |lu|me |</V>

<V>|su |la |tri|sta |ri|vie|ra |d’ a|che|ron|te |</V>
<T><V>|al|lor |con |li oc|chi |ver|go|gno|si e |bas|si |</V>

<V>|in|fi|no al |fiu|me |del |par|lar |mi |tras|si |</V>

<V>|un |vec|chio |bian|co |per |an|ti|co |pe|lo |</V>
<V>|gri|dan|do |guai |a |voi |a|ni|me |pra|ve |</V>
<T><V>|non |i|spe|ra|te |mai |ve|der |lo |cie|lo |</V>

<V>|rat|to |che ’n|te|ser |le |pa|ro|le |cru|de |</V>

<T><V>|poi |si |ri|tras|ser |tut|te |quan|te in|sie|me |</V>

<V>|giu|gnem|mo in |pra|to |di |fre|sca |ver|du|ra |</V>
<T><V>|gen|ti |v’ e|ran |con |oc|chi |tar|di e |gra|vi |</V>
<V>|di |gran|de au|to|ri|tà |ne’ |lor |sem|bian|ti |</V>
<V>|par|la|van |ra|do |con |vo|ci |so|a|vi |</V>
<T><V>|tra|em|mo|ci |co|sì |da |l’ un |de’ |can|ti |</V>
<V>|in |lo|co a|per|to |lu|mi|no|so e |al|to |</V>
<V>|sì |che |ve|der |si |po|tien |tut|ti |quan|ti |</V>
<T><V>|co|là |di|rit|to |so|vra ’l |ver|de |smal|to |</V>
<V>|mi |fuor |mo|stra|ti |li |spi|ri|ti |ma|gni |</V>
<V>|che |del |ve|de|re in |me |stes|so |m’ es|sal|to |</V>
<T><V>|i’ |vi|di e|le|tra |con |mol|ti |com|pa|gni |</V>
<V>|ce|sa|re ar|ma|to |con |li oc|chi |gri|fa|gni |</V>
<V>|da |l’ al|tra |par|te |vi|di ’l |re |la|ti|no |</V>
<T><V>|vi|di |quel |bru|to |che |cac|ciò |tar|qui|no |</V>
<V>|lu|cre|zia |iu|lia |mar|zï|a e |cor|ni|glia |</V>
<V>|e |so|lo in |par|te |vi|di ’l |sa|la|di|no |</V>
<T><V>|poi |ch’ in|nal|zai |un |po|co |più |le |ci|glia |</V>
<V>|vi|di ’l |ma|e|stro |di |co|lor |che |san|no |</V>
<V>|se|der |tra |fi|lo|so|fi|ca |fa|mi|glia |</V>
<T><V>|tut|ti |lo |mi|ran |tut|ti o|nor |li |fan|no |</V>
<V>|qui|vi |vi|d’ ï|o |so|cra|te e |pla|to|ne |</V>
<V>|che ’n|nan|zi a |li al|tri |più |pres|so |li |stan|no |</V>
<T><V>|de|mo|cri|to |che ’l |mon|do a |ca|so |po|ne |</V>

<V>|em|pe|do|clès |e|ra|cli|to e |ze|no|ne |</V>
<T><V>|e |vi|di il |buo|no ac|co|gli|tor |del |qua|le |</V>

<V>|i|po|crà|te a|vi|cen|na e |ga|lï|e|no |</V>
<T><V>|io |non |pos|so |ri|trar |di |tut|ti a |pie|no |</V>
<V>|pe|rò |che |sì |mi |cac|cia il |lun|go |te|ma |</V>
<V>|che |mol|te |vol|te al |fat|to il |dir |vien |me|no |</V>
<T><V>|per |al|tra |via |mi |me|na il |sa|vio |du|ca |</V>

<T><V>|ve|de |qual |lo|co |d’ in|fer|no è |da |es|sa |</V>

<V>|ciò |che |si |vuo|le e |più |non |di|man|da|re |</V>
<T><V>|or |in|co|min|cian |le |do|len|ti |no|te |</V>

<V>|se |da |con|tra|ri |ven|ti è |com|bat|tu|to |</V>

<T><V>|in|te|si |ch’ a |co|sì |fat|to |tor|men|to |</V>
<V>|en|no |dan|na|ti i |pec|ca|tor |car|na|li |</V>

<T><V>|co|me |tu |ve|di in |que|sto |bas|so in|fer|no |</V>
<V>|noi |pur |giu|gnem|mo |den|tro a |l’ al|te |fos|se |</V>
<V>|che |val|lan |quel|la |ter|ra |scon|so|la|ta |</V>
<T><V>|le |mu|ra |mi |pa|rean |che |fer|ro |fos|se |</V>
<V>|non |san|za |pri|ma |far |gran|de ag|gi|ra|ta |</V>
<V>|ve|nim|mo in |par|te |do|ve il |noc|chier |for|te |</V>
<T><V>|u|sci|te|ci |gri|dò |qui |è |l’ in|tra|ta |</V>
<V>|io |vi|di |più |di |mil|le in |su |le |por|te |</V>
<V>|da |ciel |pio|vu|ti |che |stiz|zo|sa|men|te |</V>
<T><V>|di|cean |chi |è |co|stui |che |san|za |mor|te |</V>

<V>|al|lor |chiu|se|ro un |po|co il |gran |di|sde|gno |</V>

<T><V>|nel |suon |de |le |pa|ro|le |ma|la|det|te |</V>

<V>|m’ a|vë|an |di |co|stui |già |let|to il |no|me |</V>
<T><V>|pe|rò |fu |la |ri|spo|sta |co|sì |pie|na |</V>
<V>|di |sù|bi|to |driz|za|to |gri|dò |co|me |</V>
<V>|di|ce|sti el|li eb|be |non |vi|v’ el|li an|co|ra |</V>
<T><V>|non |fie|re |li oc|chi |suoi |lo |dol|ce |lu|me |</V>
<V>|quan|do |s’ ac|cor|se |d’ al|cu|na |di|mo|ra |</V>
<V>|ch’ io |fa|cë|a |di|nan|zi a |la |ri|spo|sta |</V>
<T><V>|su|pin |ri|cad|de e |più |non |par|ve |fo|ra |</V>
<V>|ma |quel|l’ al|tro |ma|gna|ni|mo a |cui |po|sta |</V>
<V>|re|sta|to |m’ e|ra |non |mu|tò |a|spet|to |</V>
<T><V>|né |mos|se |col|lo |né |pie|gò |sua |co|sta |</V>

<V>|s’ el|li han |quel|l’ ar|te |dis|se |ma|le ap|pre|sa |</V>
<T><V>|ciò |mi |tor|men|ta |più |che |que|sto |let|to |</V>
<V>|ma |non |cin|quan|ta |vol|te |fia |rac|ce|sa |</V>
<V>|la |fac|cia |de |la |don|na |che |qui |reg|ge |</V>
<T><V>|che |tu |sa|prai |quan|to |quel|l’ ar|te |pe|sa |</V>

<V>|dim|mi |per|ché |quel |po|po|lo è |sì |em|pio |</V>
<T><V>|in|con|tr’ a’ |miei |in |cia|scu|na |sua |leg|ge |</V>

<V>|di|nan|zi |quel |che ’l |tem|po |se|co ad|du|ce |</V>

<V>|le |co|se |dis|se |che |ne |son |lon|ta|no |</V>
<T><V>|co|tan|to an|cor |ne |splen|de il |som|mo |du|ce |</V>

<V>|no|stro in|tel|let|to e |s’ al|tri |non |ci ap|por|ta |</V>

<T><V>|quan|do |sa|rai |di|nan|zi al |dol|ce |rag|gio |</V>

<V>|del |puz|zo |che ’l |pro|fon|do a|bis|so |git|ta |</V>

<T><V>|al |tri|sto |fia|to e |poi |no i |fia |ri|guar|do |</V>

<V>|li |fro|do|len|ti e |più |do|lor |li as|sa|le |</V>

<T><V>|nel |pros|si|mo |si |dan|no e |nel |suo a|ve|re |</V>

<V>|e |tra ’l |piè |de |la |ri|pa ed |es|sa in |trac|cia |</V>
<T><V>|cor|rien |cen|tau|ri ar|ma|ti |di |sa|et|te |</V>

<V>|veg|gen|do|ci |ca|lar |cia|scun |ri|stet|te |</V>
<T><V>|e |de |la |schie|ra |tre |si |di|par|ti|ro |</V>
<V>|con |ar|chi e |as|tic|ciuo|le |pri|ma e|let|te |</V>
<V>|e |l’ un |gri|dò |da |lun|gi a |qual |mar|ti|ro |</V>
<T><V>|ve|ni|te |voi |che |scen|de|te |la |co|sta |</V>
<V>|di|tel |co|stin|ci |se |non |l’ ar|co |ti|ro |</V>
<V>|lo |mio |ma|e|stro |dis|se |la |ri|spo|sta |</V>

<V>|che |fu |da’ |piè |di |ca|ton |già |sop|pres|sa |</V>

<T><V>|e |pa|rea |po|sta |lor |di|ver|sa |leg|ge |</V>
<V>|al|cu|na |si |se|dea |tut|ta |rac|col|ta |</V>
<V>|e |al|tra an|da|va |con|ti|nü|a|men|te |</V>
<T><V>|quel|la |che |gi|va ’n|tor|no e|ra |più |mol|ta |</V>
<V>|e |quel|la |men |che |gia|cë|a al |tor|men|to |</V>
<V>|ma |più |al |duo|lo a|vea |la |lin|gua |sciol|ta |</V>

<V>|gen|te |vien |con |la |qua|le es|ser |non |deg|gio |</V>
<V>|sie|ti |rac|co|man|da|to il |mio |te|so|ro |</V>
<T><V>|nel |qual |io |vi|vo an|co|ra e |più |non |cheg|gio |</V>
<V>|poi |si |ri|vol|se e |par|ve |di |co|lo|ro |</V>
<V>|che |cor|ro|no a |ve|ro|na il |drap|po |ver|de |</V>
<T><V>|per |la |cam|pa|gna e |par|ve |di |co|sto|ro |</V>
<V>|quel|li |che |vin|ce |non |co|lui |che |per|de |</V>
<V>|de |l’ ac|qua |che |ca|dea |ne |l’ al|tro |gi|ro |</V>
<T><V>|si|mi|le a |quel |che |l’ ar|nie |fan|no |rom|bo |</V>
<V>|quan|do |tre |om|bre in|sie|me |si |par|ti|ro |</V>
<V>|cor|ren|do |d’ u|na |tor|ma |che |pas|sa|va |</V>
<T><V>|sot|to |la |piog|gia |de |l’ a|spro |mar|ti|ro |</V>
<V>|ve|nian |ver’ |noi |e |cia|scu|na |gri|da|va |</V>
<V>|sò|sta|ti |tu |ch’ a |l’ a|bi|to |ne |sem|bri |</V>
<T><V>|es|ser |al|cun |di |no|stra |ter|ra |pra|va |</V>
<V>|ri|cen|ti e |vec|chie |da |le |fiam|me in|ce|se |</V>
<V>|an|cor |men |duol |pur |ch’ i’ |me |ne |ri|mem|bri |</V>
<T><V>|a |le |lor |gri|da il |mio |dot|tor |s’ at|te|se |</V>

<V>|dis|se a |co|stor |si |vuo|le es|ser |cor|te|se |</V>
<T><V>|e |se |non |fos|se il |fo|co |che |sa|et|ta |</V>

<V>|fu |di |gra|do |mag|gior |che |tu |non |cre|di |</V>
<V>|ne|po|te |fu |de |la |buo|na |gual|dra|da |</V>

<V>|ché |do|po |lui |ver|rà |di |più |lai|da o|pra |</V>
<V>|di |ver’ |po|nen|te un |pa|stor |san|za |leg|ge |</V>
<T><V>|tal |che |con|vien |che |lui |e |me |ri|cuo|pra |</V>

<V>|ne’ |mac|ca|bei |e |co|me a |quel |fu |mol|le |</V>
<T><V>|suo |re |co|sì |fia |lui |chi |fran|cia |reg|ge |</V>

<V>|ch’ i’ |pur |ri|spuo|si |lui |a |que|sto |me|tro |</V>

<V>|e |vol|ser |con|tra |lui |tut|t’ i |run|ci|gli |</V>
<T><V>|ma |el |gri|dò |nes|sun |di |voi |sia |fel|lo |</V>
<V>|in|nan|zi |che |l’ un|cin |vo|stro |mi |pi|gli |</V>
<V>|trag|ga|si a|van|te |l’ un |di |voi |che |m’ o|da |</V>
<T><V>|e |poi |d’ ar|run|ci|gliar|mi |si |con|si|gli |</V>
<V>|tut|ti |gri|da|ron |va|da |ma|la|co|da |</V>
<V>|per |ch’ un |si |mos|se e |li al|tri |stet|ter |fer|mi |</V>
<T><V>|e |ven|ne a |lui |di|cen|do |che |li ap|pro|da |</V>
<V>|cre|di |tu |ma|la|co|da |qui |ve|der|mi |</V>
<V>|es|ser |ve|nu|to |dis|se ’l |mio |ma|e|stro |</V>
<T><V>|si|cu|ro |già |da |tut|ti |vo|stri |scher|mi |</V>
<V>|san|za |vo|ler |di|vi|no e |fa|to |de|stro |</V>
<V>|la|scia|n’ an|dar |ché |nel |cie|lo è |vo|lu|to |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ i’ |mo|stri al|trui |que|sto |cam|min |sil|ve|stro |</V>
<V>|al|lor |li |fu |l’ or|go|glio |sì |ca|du|to |</V>
<V>|ch’ e’ |si |la|sciò |ca|scar |l’ un|ci|no a’ |pie|di |</V>
<T><V>|e |dis|se a |li al|tri o|mai |non |sia |fe|ru|to |</V>
<V>|tra |li |scheg|gion |del |pon|te |quat|to |quat|to |</V>
<V>|si|cu|ra|men|te o|mai |a |me |ti |rie|di |</V>
<T><V>|per |ch’ io |mi |mos|si e |a |lui |ven|ni |rat|to |</V>
<V>|e i |dia|vo|li |si |fe|cer |tut|ti a|van|ti |</V>
<V>|sì |ch’ io |te|met|ti |ch’ ei |te|nes|ser |pat|to |</V>
<T><V>|co|sì |vi|d’ ï|o |già |te|mer |li |fan|ti |</V>
<V>|ch’ u|sci|van |pat|teg|gia|ti |di |ca|pro|na |</V>
<V>|veg|gen|do |sé |tra |ne|mi|ci |co|tan|ti |</V>
<T><V>|i’ |m’ ac|co|stai |con |tut|ta |la |per|so|na |</V>
<V>|lun|go ’l |mio |du|ca e |non |tor|ce|va |li oc|chi |</V>
<V>|da |la |sem|bian|za |lor |ch’ e|ra |non |buo|na |</V>
<T><V>|ei |chi|na|van |li |raf|fi e |vuo’ |che ’l |toc|chi |</V>
<V>|di|ce|va |l’ un |con |l’ al|tro in |sul |grop|po|ne |</V>
<V>|e |ri|spon|dien |sì |fa |che |glie|l’ ac|coc|chi |</V>
<T><V>|ma |quel |de|mo|nio |che |te|nea |ser|mo|ne |</V>
<V>|col |du|ca |mio |si |vol|se |tut|to |pre|sto |</V>
<V>|e |dis|se |po|sa |po|sa |scar|mi|glio|ne |</V>
<T><V>|poi |dis|se a |noi |più |ol|tre an|dar |per |que|sto |</V>
<V>|i|sco|glio |non |si |può |pe|rò |che |gia|ce |</V>
<V>|tut|to |spez|za|to al |fon|do |l’ ar|co |se|sto |</V>
<T><V>|e |se |l’ an|da|re a|van|te |pur |vi |pia|ce |</V>
<V>|an|da|te|ve|ne |su |per |que|sta |grot|ta |</V>
<V>|pres|so è |un |al|tro |sco|glio |che |via |fa|ce |</V>
<T><V>|ier |più |ol|tre |cin|qu’ o|re |che |que|st’ ot|ta |</V>
<V>|an|ni |com|pié |che |qui |la |via |fu |rot|ta |</V>
<V>|a |ri|guar|dar |s’ al|cun |se |ne |scio|ri|na |</V>
<T><V>|tra’ |ti a|van|te a|li|chi|no e |cal|ca|bri|na |</V>
<V>|co|min|ciò |el|li a |di|re e |tu |ca|gnaz|zo |</V>
<V>|e |bar|ba|ric|cia |gui|di |la |de|ci|na |</V>
<T><V>|ci|rï|at|to |san|nu|to e |graf|fia|ca|ne |</V>
<V>|e |far|fa|rel|lo e |ru|bi|can|te |paz|zo |</V>
<V>|cer|ca|te ’n|tor|no |le |bo|glien|ti |pa|ne |</V>
<T><V>|co|stor |sian |sal|vi in|fi|no a |l’ al|tro |scheg|gio |</V>
<V>|che |tut|to in|te|ro |va |so|vra |le |ta|ne |</V>
<V>|o|mè |ma|e|stro |che |è |quel |ch’ i’ |veg|gio |</V>
<T><V>|dis|s’ io |deh |san|za |scor|ta an|dian|ci |so|li |</V>
<V>|se |tu |sa’ |ir |ch’ i’ |per |me |non |la |cheg|gio |</V>
<V>|se |tu |se’ |sì |ac|cor|to |co|me |suo|li |</V>
<T><V>|non |ve|di |tu |ch’ e’ |di|gri|gnan |li |den|ti |</V>
<V>|e |con |le |ci|glia |ne |mi|nac|cian |duo|li |</V>
<V>|ed |el|li a |me |non |vo’ |che |tu |pa|ven|ti |</V>
<T><V>|la|scia|li |di|gri|gnar |pur |a |lor |sen|no |</V>
<V>|ch’ e’ |fan|no |ciò |per |li |les|si |do|len|ti |</V>
<V>|per |l’ ar|gi|ne |si|ni|stro |vol|ta |dien|no |</V>
<T><V>|ma |pri|ma a|vea |cia|scun |la |lin|gua |stret|ta |</V>
<V>|coi |den|ti |ver|so |lor |du|ca |per |cen|no |</V>
<V>|ed |el|li a|vea |del |cul |fat|to |trom|bet|ta |</V>
<T><V>|io |vi|di |già |ca|va|lier |muo|ver |cam|po |</V>

<V>|e |tal|vol|ta |par|tir |per |lo|ro |scam|po |</V>
<T><V>|cor|ri|dor |vi|di |per |la |ter|ra |vo|stra |</V>

<V>|con |tam|bu|ri e |con |cen|ni |di |ca|stel|la |</V>
<T><V>|e |con |co|se |no|stra|li e |con |i|stra|ne |</V>
<V>|né |già |con |sì |di|ver|sa |cen|na|mel|la |</V>
<V>|ca|va|lier |vi|di |muo|ver |né |pe|do|ni |</V>
<T><V>|né |na|ve a |se|gno |di |ter|ra o |di |stel|la |</V>
<V>|noi |an|da|vam |con |li |die|ce |de|mo|ni |</V>
<V>|ahi |fie|ra |com|pa|gnia |ma |ne |la |chie|sa |</V>
<T><V>|coi |san|ti e |in |ta|ver|na |coi |ghiot|to|ni |</V>
<V>|pur |a |la |pe|go|la e|ra |la |mia ’n|te|sa |</V>
<V>|per |ve|der |de |la |bol|gia o|gne |con|te|gno |</V>
<T><V>|e |de |la |gen|te |ch’ en|tro |v’ e|ra in|ce|sa |</V>
<V>|co|me i |dal|fi|ni |quan|do |fan|no |se|gno |</V>
<V>|a’ |ma|ri|nar |con |l’ ar|co |de |la |schie|na |</V>
<T><V>|che |s’ ar|go|men|tin |di |cam|par |lor |le|gno |</V>
<V>|ta|lor |co|sì |ad |al|leg|giar |la |pe|na |</V>
<V>|mo|stra|v’ al|cun |de’ |pec|ca|to|ri ’l |dos|so |</V>
<T><V>|e |co|me a |l’ or|lo |de |l’ ac|qua |d’ un |fos|so |</V>
<V>|stan|no i |ra|noc|chi |pur |col |mu|so |fuo|ri |</V>
<V>|sì |che |ce|la|no i |pie|di e |l’ al|tro |gros|so |</V>
<T><V>|sì |sta|van |d’ o|gne |par|te i |pec|ca|to|ri |</V>

<V>|co|sì |si |ri|tra|én |sot|to i |bol|lo|ri |</V>

<V>|ch’ u|na |ra|na |ri|ma|ne e |l’ al|tra |spic|cia |</V>
<T><V>|e |graf|fia|can |che |li e|ra |più |di |con|tra |</V>

<V>|e |tras|sel |sù |che |mi |par|ve u|na |lon|tra |</V>

<V>|e |poi |ch’ e’ |si |chia|ma|ro at|te|si |co|me |</V>

<V>|gri|da|van |tut|ti in|sie|me i |ma|la|det|ti |</V>
<V>|che |tu |sap|pi |chi |è |lo |scia|gu|ra|to |</V>
<T><V>|lo |du|ca |mio |li |s’ ac|co|stò |al|la|to |</V>

<V>|i’ |fui |del |re|gno |di |na|var|ra |na|to |</V>
<T><V>|mia |ma|dre a |ser|vo |d’ un |se|gnor |mi |puo|se |</V>

<V>|di|strug|gi|tor |di |sé |e |di |sue |co|se |</V>
<T><V>|poi |fui |fa|mi|glia |del |buon |re |te|bal|do |</V>

<V>|d’ o|gne |par|te u|na |san|na |co|me a |por|co |</V>
<T><V>|tra |ma|le |gat|te e|ra |ve|nu|to ’l |sor|co |</V>

<V>|e |dis|se |sta|te in |là |men|tr’ io |lo ’n|for|co |</V>
<T><V>|e |al |ma|e|stro |mio |vol|se |la |fac|cia |</V>

<T><V>|a|ven|do |più |di |lui |che |di |sé |cu|ra |</V>
<V>|tan|to |che |so|lo u|na |ca|mi|scia |ve|sta |</V>
<V>|e |giù |dal |col|lo |de |la |ri|pa |du|ra |</V>
<T><V>|su|pin |si |die|de a |la |pen|den|te |roc|cia |</V>
<V>|che |l’ un |de’ |la|ti a |l’ al|tra |bol|gia |tu|ra |</V>
<V>|non |cor|se |mai |sì |to|sto ac|qua |per |doc|cia |</V>
<T><V>|a |vol|ger |ruo|ta |di |mo|lin |ter|ra|gno |</V>

<V>|co|me ’l |ma|e|stro |mio |per |quel |vi|va|gno |</V>
<T><V>|por|tan|do|se|ne |me |so|vra ’l |suo |pet|to |</V>
<V>|co|me |suo |fi|glio |non |co|me |com|pa|gno |</V>
<V>|a |pe|na |fuo|ro i |piè |suoi |giun|ti al |let|to |</V>

<V>|e |det|to |l’ ho |per|ché |do|ler |ti |deb|bia |</V>
<V>|al |fi|ne |de |le |sue |pa|ro|le il |la|dro |</V>
<T><V>|le |ma|ni al|zò |con |a|men|due |le |fi|che |</V>

<V>|da |in|di in |qua |mi |fuor |le |ser|pi a|mi|che |</V>
<T><V>|per|ch’ u|na |li |s’ av|vol|se al|lo|ra al |col|lo |</V>

<V>|e |u|n’ al|tra a |le |brac|cia e |ri|le|gol|lo |</V>
<T><V>|ri|ba|den|do |sé |stes|sa |sì |di|nan|zi |</V>

<V>|ahi |pi|sto|ia |pi|sto|ia |ché |non |stan|zi |</V>

<V>|vin|cer |po|te|ro |den|tro a |me |l’ ar|do|re |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ i’ |eb|bi a |di|ve|nir |del |mon|do e|sper|to |</V>
<V>|e |de |li |vi|zi u|ma|ni e |del |va|lo|re |</V>
<V>|ma |mi|si |me |per |l’ al|to |ma|re a|per|to |</V>
<T><V>|sol |con |un |le|gno e |con |quel|la |com|pa|gna |</V>
<V>|pic|cio|la |da |la |qual |non |fui |di|ser|to |</V>
<V>|l’ un |li|to e |l’ al|tro |vi|di in|fin |la |spa|gna |</V>
<T><V>|fin |nel |mor|roc|co e |l’ i|so|la |d’ i |sar|di |</V>
<V>|e |l’ al|tre |che |quel |ma|re in|tor|no |ba|gna |</V>
<V>|io |e ’ |com|pa|gni e|ra|vam |vec|chi e |tar|di |</V>
<T><V>|quan|do |ve|nim|mo a |quel|la |fo|ce |stret|ta |</V>
<V>|do|v’ er|cu|le |seg|nò |li |suoi |ri|guar|di |</V>
<V>|ac|ciò |che |l’ uom |più |ol|tre |non |si |met|ta |</V>

<V>|o |fra|ti |dis|si |che |per |cen|to |mi|lia |</V>
<T><V>|pe|ri|gli |sie|te |giun|ti a |l’ oc|ci|den|te |</V>

<T><V>|non |vo|glia|te |ne|gar |l’ e|spe|rï|en|za |</V>

<T><V>|fat|ti |non |fo|ste a |vi|ver |co|me |bru|ti |</V>

<V>|ri|mem|bri|ti |di |pier |da |me|di|ci|na |</V>
<T><V>|se |mai |tor|ni a |ve|der |lo |dol|ce |pia|no |</V>
<V>|che |da |ver|cel|li a |mar|ca|bò |di|chi|na |</V>
<V>|e |fa |sa|per |a’ |due |mi|glior |da |fa|no |</V>
<T><V>|a |mes|ser |gui|do e |an|co ad |an|gio|lel|lo |</V>
<V>|che |se |l’ an|ti|ve|der |qui |non |è |va|no |</V>
<V>|git|ta|ti |sa|ran |fuor |di |lor |va|sel|lo |</V>
<T><V>|per |tra|di|men|to |d’ un |ti|ran|no |fel|lo |</V>
<V>|non |vi|de |mai |sì |gran |fal|lo |net|tu|no |</V>
<V>|quel |tra|di|tor |che |ve|de |pur |con |l’ u|no |</V>
<T><V>|e |tien |la |ter|ra |che |ta|le |qui |me|co |</V>
<V>|vor|reb|be |di |ve|de|re es|ser |di|giu|no |</V>
<V>|fa|rà |ve|nir|li a |par|la|men|to |se|co |</V>
<T><V>|poi |fa|rà |sì |ch’ al |ven|to |di |fo|ca|ra |</V>

<V>|e |io |a |lui |di|mo|stra|mi e |di|chia|ra |</V>
<T><V>|se |vuo’ |ch’ i’ |por|ti |sù |di |te |no|vel|la |</V>

<V>|al|lor |puo|se |la |ma|no a |la |ma|scel|la |</V>

<V>|fal|si|fi|can|do |sé |in |al|trui |for|ma |</V>
<V>|co|me |l’ al|tro |che |là |sen |va |so|sten|ne |</V>
<T><V>|per |gua|da|gnar |la |don|na |de |la |tor|ma |</V>
<V>|fal|si|fi|ca|re in |sé |buo|so |do|na|ti |</V>
<V>|te|stan|do e |dan|do al |te|sta|men|to |nor|ma |</V>
<T><V>|e |poi |che i |due |rab|bio|si |fuor |pas|sa|ti |</V>
<V>|so|vra |cu’ |io |a|vea |l’ oc|chio |te|nu|to |</V>
<V>|ri|vol|si|lo a |guar|dar |li al|tri |mal |na|ti |</V>
<T><V>|io |vi|di un |fat|to a |gui|sa |di |lë|u|to |</V>
<V>|pur |ch’ el|li a|ves|se a|vu|ta |l’ an|gui|na|ia |</V>
<V>|tron|ca |da |l’ al|tro |che |l’ uo|mo ha |for|cu|to |</V>
<T><V>|la |gra|ve i|dro|pe|sì |che |sì |di|spa|ia |</V>
<V>|le |mem|bra |con |l’ o|mor |che |mal |con|ver|te |</V>
<V>|che ’l |vi|so |non |ri|spon|de a |la |ven|tra|ia |</V>
<T><V>|fa|ce|va |lui |te|ner |le |lab|bra a|per|te |</V>
<V>|co|me |l’ e|ti|co |fa |che |per |la |se|te |</V>
<V>|l’ un |ver|so ’l |men|to e |l’ al|tro in |sù |rin|ver|te |</V>
<T><V>|o |voi |che |san|z’ al|cu|na |pe|na |sie|te |</V>
<V>|e |non |so |io |per|ché |nel |mon|do |gra|mo |</V>
<V>|dis|s’ el|li a |noi |guar|da|te e |at|ten|de|te |</V>
<T><V>|a |la |mi|se|ria |del |ma|e|stro a|da|mo |</V>
<V>|io |eb|bi |vi|vo as|sai |di |quel |ch’ i’ |vol|li |</V>
<V>|e |o|ra |las|so un |goc|ciol |d’ ac|qua |bra|mo |</V>
<T><V>|li |ru|scel|let|ti |che |d’ i |ver|di |col|li |</V>
<V>|del |ca|sen|tin |di|scen|don |giu|so in |ar|no |</V>
<V>|fac|cen|do i |lor |ca|na|li |fred|di e |mol|li |</V>
<T><V>|sem|pre |mi |stan|no in|nan|zi e |non |in|dar|no |</V>
<V>|ché |l’ i|ma|gi|ne |lor |vie |più |m’ a|sciu|ga |</V>
<V>|che ’l |ma|le on|d’ io |nel |vol|to |mi |di|scar|no |</V>
<T><V>|la |ri|gi|da |giu|sti|zia |che |mi |fru|ga |</V>
<V>|a |met|ter |più |li |miei |so|spi|ri in |fu|ga |</V>
<V>|la |le|ga |sug|gel|la|ta |del |ba|ti|sta |</V>
<T><V>|ma |s’ io |ve|des|si |qui |l’ a|ni|ma |tri|sta |</V>
<V>|di |gui|do o |d’ a|les|san|dro o |di |lor |fra|te |</V>
<V>|per |fon|te |bran|da |non |da|rei |la |vi|sta |</V>
<T><V>|den|tro |c’ è |l’ u|na |già |se |l’ ar|rab|bia|te |</V>
<V>|om|bre |che |van|no in|tor|no |di|con |ve|ro |</V>
<V>|ma |che |mi |val |c’ ho |le |mem|bra |le|ga|te |</V>
<T><V>|s’ io |fos|si |pur |di |tan|to an|cor |leg|ge|ro |</V>
<V>|ch’ i’ |po|tes|si in |cen|t’ an|ni an|da|re u|n’ on|cia |</V>
<V>|io |sa|rei |mes|so |già |per |lo |sen|tie|ro |</V>
<T><V>|cer|can|do |lui |tra |que|sta |gen|te |scon|cia |</V>
<V>|con |tut|to |ch’ el|la |vol|ge un|di|ci |mi|glia |</V>
<V>|e |men |d’ un |mez|zo |di |tra|ver|so |non |ci ha |</V>
<T><V>|io |son |per |lor |tra |sì |fat|ta |fa|mi|glia |</V>
<V>|e’ |m’ in|dus|se|ro a |bat|ter |li |fio|ri|ni |</V>
<V>|ch’ a|ve|van |tre |ca|ra|ti |di |mon|di|glia |</V>
<T><V>|e |io |a |lui |chi |son |li |due |ta|pi|ni |</V>
<V>|che |fum|man |co|me |man |ba|gna|te ’l |ver|no |</V>
<V>|gia|cen|do |stret|ti a’ |tuoi |de|stri |con|fi|ni |</V>
<T><V>|qui |li |tro|vai |e |poi |vol|ta |non |dier|no |</V>
<V>|ri|spuo|se |quan|do |piov|vi in |que|sto |grep|po |</V>
<V>|e |non |cre|do |che |die|no in |sem|pi|ter|no |</V>
<T><V>|l’ u|na è |la |fal|sa |ch’ ac|cu|sò |gio|sep|po |</V>
<V>|l’ al|tr’ è ’l |fal|so |si|non |gre|co |di |tro|ia |</V>
<V>|per |feb|bre a|gu|ta |git|tan |tan|to |lep|po |</V>
<T><V>|e |l’ un |di |lor |che |si |re|cò |a |no|ia |</V>
<V>|for|se |d’ es|ser |no|ma|to |sì |o|scu|ro |</V>
<V>|col |pu|gno |li |per|cos|se |l’ e|pa |cro|ia |</V>
<T><V>|quel|la |so|nò |co|me |fos|se un |tam|bu|ro |</V>
<V>|e |ma|stro a|da|mo |li |per|cos|se il |vol|to |</V>
<V>|col |brac|cio |suo |che |non |par|ve |men |du|ro |</V>
<T><V>|di|cen|do a |lui |an|cor |che |mi |sia |tol|to |</V>
<V>|lo |muo|ver |per |le |mem|bra |che |son |gra|vi |</V>
<V>|on|d’ ei |ri|spuo|se |quan|do |tu |an|da|vi |</V>
<T><V>|al |fuo|co |non |l’ a|vei |tu |co|sì |pre|sto |</V>
<V>|ma |sì |e |più |l’ a|vei |quan|do |co|nia|vi |</V>
<V>|e |l’ i|dro|pi|co |tu |di’ |ver |di |que|sto |</V>
<T><V>|ma |tu |non |fo|sti |sì |ver |te|sti|mo|nio |</V>
<V>|là |’ve |del |ver |fo|sti a |tro|ia |ri|che|sto |</V>
<V>|s’ io |dis|si |fal|so e |tu |fal|sa|sti il |co|nio |</V>
<T><V>|e |tu |per |più |ch’ al|cun |al|tro |de|mo|nio |</V>
<V>|ri|cor|di|ti |sper|giu|ro |del |ca|val|lo |</V>
<V>|ri|spuo|se |quel |ch’ a|vë|a in|fia|ta |l’ e|pa |</V>
<T><V>|e |sie|ti |reo |che |tut|to il |mon|do |sal|lo |</V>
<V>|e |te |sia |rea |la |se|te on|de |ti |cre|pa |</V>
<V>|dis|se ’l |gre|co |la |lin|gua e |l’ ac|qua |mar|cia |</V>
<T><V>|che ’l |ven|tre in|nan|zi a |li oc|chi |sì |t’ as|sie|pa |</V>
<V>|al|lo|ra il |mo|ne|tier |co|sì |si |squar|cia |</V>
<V>|la |boc|ca |tua |per |tuo |mal |co|me |suo|le |</V>
<T><V>|ché |s’ i’ |ho |se|te e |o|mor |mi |rin|far|cia |</V>
<V>|tu |hai |l’ ar|su|ra e ’l |ca|po |che |ti |duo|le |</V>
<V>|e |per |lec|car |lo |spec|chio |di |nar|cis|so |</V>
<T><V>|non |vor|re|sti a ’n|vi|tar |mol|te |pa|ro|le |</V>
<V>|quan|do ’l |ma|e|stro |mi |dis|se or |pur |mi|ra |</V>
<V>|che |per |po|co |che |te|co |non |mi |ris|so |</V>
<T><V>|quan|d’ io ’l |sen|ti’ |a |me |par|lar |con |i|ra |</V>
<V>|vol|si|mi |ver|so |lui |con |tal |ver|go|gna |</V>
<V>|ch’ an|cor |per |la |me|mo|ria |mi |si |gi|ra |</V>
<T><V>|qual |è |co|lui |che |suo |dan|nag|gio |so|gna |</V>
<V>|che |so|gnan|do |de|si|de|ra |so|gna|re |</V>
<V>|sì |che |quel |ch’ è |co|me |non |fos|se a|go|gna |</V>
<T><V>|tal |mi |fe|c’ io |non |pos|sen|do |par|la|re |</V>
<V>|che |di|sï|a|va |scu|sar|mi e |scu|sa|va |</V>
<V>|mag|gior |di|fet|to |men |ver|go|gna |la|va |</V>
<T><V>|dis|se ’l |ma|e|stro |che ’l |tuo |non |è |sta|to |</V>
<V>|pe|rò |d’ o|gne |tre|sti|zia |ti |di|sgra|va |</V>
<V>|e |fa |ra|gion |ch’ io |ti |sia |sem|pre al|la|to |</V>
<T><V>|se |più |av|vien |che |for|tu|na |t’ ac|co|glia |</V>

<V>|ché |vo|ler |ciò |u|di|re è |bas|sa |vo|glia |</V>

<V>|sì |che |mi |tin|se |l’ u|na e |l’ al|tra |guan|cia |</V>
<V>|e |poi |la |me|di|ci|na |mi |ri|por|se |</V>
<T><V>|co|sì |o|d’ io |che |so|lea |far |la |lan|cia |</V>

<V>|pri|ma |di |tri|sta e |poi |di |buo|na |man|cia |</V>
<T><V>|noi |dem|mo il |dos|so al |mi|se|ro |val|lo|ne |</V>
<V>|su |per |la |ri|pa |che ’l |cin|ge |din|tor|no |</V>
<V>|at|tra|ver|san|do |san|za al|cun |ser|mo|ne |</V>
<T><V>|qui|v’ e|ra |men |che |not|te e |men |che |gior|no |</V>
<V>|sì |che ’l |vi|so |m’ an|da|va in|nan|zi |po|co |</V>
<V>|ma |io |sen|ti’ |so|na|re un |al|to |cor|no |</V>
<T><V>|tan|to |ch’ av|reb|be o|gne |tuon |fat|to |fio|co |</V>

<V>|di|riz|zò |li oc|chi |miei |tut|ti ad |un |lo|co |</V>
<T><V>|do|po |la |do|lo|ro|sa |rot|ta |quan|do |</V>
<V>|car|lo |ma|gno |per|dé |la |san|ta |ge|sta |</V>
<V>|non |so|nò |sì |ter|ri|bil|men|te or|lan|do |</V>
<T><V>|po|co |por|tä|i in |là |vol|ta |la |te|sta |</V>
<V>|che |me |par|ve |ve|der |mol|te al|te |tor|ri |</V>
<V>|on|d’ io |ma|e|stro |dì |che |ter|ra è |que|sta |</V>
<T><V>|ed |el|li a |me |pe|rò |che |tu |tra|scor|ri |</V>
<V>|per |le |te|ne|bre |trop|po |da |la |lun|gi |</V>
<V>|av|vien |che |poi |nel |ma|gi|na|re ab|bor|ri |</V>

<T><V>|né |sì |chi|na|to |lì |fe|ce |di|mo|ra |</V>
<V>|s’ ï|o a|ves|si |le |ri|me a|s|pre e |chioc|ce |</V>
<V>|co|me |si |con|ver|reb|be al |tri|sto |bu|co |</V>
<T><V>|so|vra ’l |qual |pon|tan |tut|te |l’ al|tre |roc|ce |</V>
<V>|io |pre|me|rei |di |mio |con|cet|to il |su|co |</V>
<V>|più |pie|na|men|te |ma |per|ch’ io |non |l’ ab|bo |</V>
<T><V>|non |san|za |te|ma a |di|cer |mi |con|du|co |</V>
<V>|ché |non |è im|pre|sa |da |pi|glia|re a |gab|bo |</V>
<V>|di|scri|ver |fon|do a |tut|to |l’ u|ni|ver|so |</V>
<T><V>|né |da |lin|gua |che |chia|mi |mam|ma o |bab|bo |</V>
<V>|ma |quel|le |don|ne a|iu|ti|no il |mio |ver|so |</V>
<V>|ch’ a|iu|ta|ro an|fï|o|ne a |chiu|der |te|be |</V>
<T><V>|sì |che |dal |fat|to il |dir |non |sia |di|ver|so |</V>
<V>|oh |so|vra |tut|te |mal |cre|a|ta |ple|be |</V>
<V>|che |stai |nel |lo|co on|de |par|la|re è |du|ro |</V>
<T><V>|mei |fo|ste |sta|te |qui |pe|co|re o |ze|be |</V>
<V>|co|me |noi |fum|mo |giù |nel |poz|zo |scu|ro |</V>
<V>|sot|to i |piè |del |gi|gan|te as|sai |più |bas|si |</V>
<T><V>|e |io |mi|ra|va an|co|ra a |l’ al|to |mu|ro |</V>
<V>|di|ce|re u|di’ |mi |guar|da |co|me |pas|si |</V>
<V>|va |sì |che |tu |non |cal|chi |con |le |pian|te |</V>
<T><V>|le |te|ste |de’ |fra|tei |mi|se|ri |las|si |</V>

<T><V>|o|gnu|na in |giù |te|nea |vol|ta |la |fac|cia |</V>

<V>|li oc|chi |lor |ch’ e|ran |pria |pur |den|tro |mol|li |</V>

<T><V>|di |mon|ta|per|ti |per|ché |mi |mo|le|ste |</V>

<V>|fu |mia |ri|spo|sta |se |di|man|di |fa|ma |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ io |met|ta il |no|me |tuo |tra |l’ al|tre |no|te |</V>

<T><V>|o |che |ca|pel |qui |sù |non |ti |ri|ma|gna |</V>

<V>|un |po|co |pria |che ’l |pian|to |si |rag|ge|li |</V>
<V>|per |ch’ io |a |lui |se |vuo’ |ch’ i’ |ti |sov|ve|gna |</V>
<T><V>|dim|mi |chi |se’ |e |s’ io |non |ti |di|sbri|go |</V>
<V>|al |fon|do |de |la |ghiac|cia ir |mi |con|ve|gna |</V>
<V>|ri|spuo|se a|dun|que i’ |son |fra|te al|be|ri|go |</V>
<T><V>|i’ |son |quel |da |le |frut|ta |del |mal |or|to |</V>
<V>|che |qui |ri|pren|do |dat|te|ro |per |fi|go |</V>
<V>|oh |dis|s’ io |lui |or |se’ |tu |an|cor |mor|to |</V>
<T><V>|nel |mon|do |sù |nul|la |scï|en|za |por|to |</V>
<V>|che |spes|se |vol|te |l’ a|ni|ma |ci |ca|de |</V>
<V>|e |per|ché |tu |più |vo|len|tier |mi |ra|de |</V>
<T><V>|le ’n|ve|trï|a|te |la|gri|me |dal |vol|to |</V>
<V>|sap|pie |che |to|sto |che |l’ a|ni|ma |tra|de |</V>
<V>|co|me |fe|c’ ï|o il |cor|po |suo |l’ è |tol|to |</V>
<T><V>|da |un |de|mo|nio |che |po|scia il |go|ver|na |</V>
<V>|men|tre |che ’l |tem|po |suo |tut|to |sia |vòl|to |</V>
<V>|el|la |ru|i|na in |sì |fat|ta |ci|ster|na |</V>
<T><V>|e |for|se |pa|re an|cor |lo |cor|po |su|so |</V>
<V>|de |l’ om|bra |che |di |qua |die|tro |mi |ver|na |</V>
<V>|tu ’l |dei |sa|per |se |tu |vien |pur |mo |giu|so |</V>
<T><V>|el|li è |ser |bran|ca |do|ria e |son |più |an|ni |</V>
<V>|po|scia |pas|sa|ti |ch’ el |fu |sì |rac|chiu|so |</V>
<V>|io |cre|do |dis|s’ io |lui |che |tu |m’ in|gan|ni |</V>
<T><V>|ché |bran|ca |do|ria |non |mo|rì |un|quan|che |</V>

<V>|nel |fos|so |sù |dis|s’ el |de’ |ma|le|bran|che |</V>
<T><V>|là |do|ve |bol|le |la |te|na|ce |pe|ce |</V>

<T><V>|nel |cor|po |suo |ed |un |suo |pros|si|ma|no |</V>

<V>|ma |di|sten|di og|gi|mai |in |qua |la |ma|no |</V>
<T><V>|a|pri|mi |li oc|chi e |io |non |glie|l’ a|per|si |</V>
<V>|e |cor|te|sia |fu |lui |es|ser |vil|la|no |</V>
<V>|d’ o|gne |co|stu|me e |pien |d’ o|gne |ma|ga|gna |</V>

<V>|tro|vai |di |voi |un |tal |che |per |sua |o|pra |</V>
<T><V>|in |a|ni|ma in |co|ci|to |già |si |ba|gna |</V>

<V>|ve|xil|la |re|gis |pro|de|unt |in|fer|ni |</V>
<T><V>|ver|so |di |noi |pe|rò |di|nan|zi |mi|ra |</V>

<V>|ve|der |mi |par|ve un |tal |di|fi|cio al|lot|ta |</V>
<T><V>|poi |per |lo |ven|to |mi |ri|strin|si |re|tro |</V>

<V>|al|tre |so|no a |gia|ce|re al|tre |stan|no er|te |</V>

<V>|quan|do |noi |fum|mo |fat|ti |tan|to a|van|te |</V>

<V>|d’ in|nan|zi |mi |si |tol|se e |fé |re|star|mi |</V>
<T><V>|ec|co |di|te |di|cen|do ed |ec|co il |lo|co |</V>
<V>|o|ve |con|vien |che |di |for|tez|za |t’ ar|mi |</V>
<V>|com’ |io |di|ven|ni al|lor |ge|la|to e |fio|co |</V>
<T><V>|nol |di|man|dar |let|tor |ch’ i’ |non |lo |scri|vo |</V>
<V>|pe|rò |ch’ o|gne |par|lar |sa|reb|be |po|co |</V>
<V>|io |non |mo|ri’ |e |non |ri|ma|si |vi|vo |</V>
<T><V>|pen|sa og|gi|mai |per |te |s’ hai |fior |d’ in|ge|gno |</V>

<V>|lo ’m|pe|ra|dor |del |do|lo|ro|so |re|gno |</V>
<T><V>|da |mez|zo ’l |pet|to u|scia |fuor |de |la |ghiac|cia |</V>

<T><V>|ve|di og|gi|mai |quan|t’ es|ser |dee |quel |tut|to |</V>

<V>|quel |che |pen|de |dal |ne|ro |cef|fo è |bru|to |</V>

<V>|qui|vi |tro|vam|mo |la |roc|cia |sì |er|ta |</V>
<V>|che ’n|dar|no |vi |sa|rien |le |gam|be |pron|te |</V>
<T><V>|tra |le|ri|ce e |tur|bìa |la |più |di|ser|ta |</V>
<V>|la |più |rot|ta |ru|i|na è |u|na |sca|la |</V>
<V>|ver|so |di |quel|la a|ge|vo|le e |a|per|ta |</V>

<T><V>|pun|to |non |fu |da |me |guar|da|re |sciol|ta |</V>

<V>|truo|vi |nel |tuo |ar|bi|trio |tan|ta |ce|ra |</V>
<T><V>|quan|t’ è |me|stie|re in|fi|no al |som|mo |smal|to |</V>
<V>|co|min|ciò |el|la |se |no|vel|la |ve|ra |</V>
<V>|di |val |di |ma|gra o |di |par|te |vi|ci|na |</V>
<T><V>|sai |dil|lo a |me |che |già |gran|de |là |e|ra |</V>
<V>|fui |chia|ma|to |cur|ra|do |ma|la|spi|na |</V>
<V>|non |son |l’ an|ti|co |ma |di |lui |di|sce|si |</V>
<T><V>|a’ |miei |por|tai |l’ a|mor |che |qui |raf|fi|na |</V>
<V>|oh |dis|s’ io |lui |per |li |vo|stri |pa|e|si |</V>
<V>|già |mai |non |fui |ma |do|ve |si |di|mo|ra |</V>
<T><V>|per |tut|ta eu|ro|pa |ch’ ei |non |sien |pa|le|si |</V>
<V>|la |fa|ma |che |la |vo|stra |ca|sa o|no|ra |</V>
<V>|gri|da i |se|gno|ri e |gri|da |la |con|tra|da |</V>
<T><V>|sì |che |ne |sa |chi |non |vi |fu |an|co|ra |</V>
<V>|e |io |vi |giu|ro |s’ io |di |so|pra |va|da |</V>
<V>|che |vo|stra |gen|te on|ra|ta |non |si |sfre|gia |</V>
<T><V>|del |pre|gio |de |la |bor|sa e |de |la |spa|da |</V>
<V>|u|so e |na|tu|ra |sì |la |pri|vi|le|gia |</V>
<V>|che |per|ché il |ca|po |reo |il |mon|do |tor|ca |</V>
<T><V>|so|la |va |drit|ta e ’l |mal |cam|min |di|spre|gia |</V>
<V>|ed |el|li or |va |che ’l |sol |non |si |ri|cor|ca |</V>
<V>|set|te |vol|te |nel |let|to |che ’l |mon|to|ne |</V>
<T><V>|con |tut|ti e |quat|tro i |piè |cuo|pre e |in|for|ca |</V>
<V>|che |co|te|sta |cor|te|se op|pi|nï|o|ne |</V>
<V>|ti |fia |chia|va|ta in |mez|zo |de |la |te|sta |</V>
<T><V>|con |mag|gior |chio|vi |che |d’ al|trui |ser|mo|ne |</V>
<V>|se |cor|so |di |giu|di|cio |non |s’ ar|re|sta |</V>
<V>|la |con|cu|bi|na |di |ti|to|ne an|ti|co |</V>
<T><V>|già |s’ im|bian|ca|va al |bal|co |d’ o|rï|en|te |</V>
<V>|fuor |de |le |brac|cia |del |suo |dol|ce a|mi|co |</V>
<V>|di |gem|me |la |sua |fron|te e|ra |lu|cen|te |</V>
<T><V>|po|ste in |fi|gu|ra |del |fred|do a|ni|ma|le |</V>

<V>|e |la |not|te |de’ |pas|si |con |che |sa|le |</V>
<T><V>|fat|ti a|vea |due |nel |lo|co o|v’ e|ra|va|mo |</V>
<V>|e ’l |ter|zo |già |chi|na|va in |giu|so |l’ a|le |</V>
<V>|quan|d’ io |che |me|co a|vea |di |quel |d’ a|da|mo |</V>
<T><V>|là |’ve |già |tut|ti e |cin|que |se|da|va|mo |</V>
<V>|la |ron|di|nel|la |pres|so a |la |mat|ti|na |</V>
<V>|e |che |la |men|te |no|stra |pe|re|gri|na |</V>
<T><V>|più |da |la |car|ne e |men |da’ |pen|sier |pre|sa |</V>
<V>|a |le |sue |vi|sï|on |qua|si è |di|vi|na |</V>
<V>|in |so|gno |mi |pa|rea |ve|der |so|spe|sa |</V>
<T><V>|u|n’ a|gu|glia |nel |ciel |con |pen|ne |d’ o|ro |</V>

<V>|ed |es|ser |mi |pa|rea |là |do|ve |fuo|ro |</V>
<T><V>|ab|ban|do|na|ti i |suoi |da |ga|ni|me|de |</V>

<V>|fra |me |pen|sa|va |for|se |que|sta |fie|de |</V>
<T><V>|pur |qui |per |u|so e |for|se |d’ al|tro |lo|co |</V>
<V>|di|sde|gna |di |por|tar|ne |su|so in |pie|de |</V>
<V>|poi |mi |pa|rea |che |poi |ro|ta|ta un |po|co |</V>
<T><V>|ter|ri|bil |co|me |fol|gor |di|scen|des|se |</V>

<V>|i|vi |pa|rea |che |el|la e |io |ar|des|se |</V>
<T><V>|e |sì |lo ’n|cen|dio i|ma|gi|na|to |cos|se |</V>

<V>|non |al|tri|men|ti a|chil|le |si |ri|scos|se |</V>

<T><V>|mi |fug|gì ’l |son|no e |di|ven|ta’ |i|smor|to |</V>

<V>|dal|la|to |m’ e|ra |so|lo il |mio |con|for|to |</V>
<T><V>|e ’l |so|le e|r’ al|to |già |più |che |due |o|re |</V>

<V>|non |a|ver |te|ma |dis|se il |mio |se|gno|re |</V>
<T><V>|fat|ti |si|cur |ché |noi |se|mo a |buon |pun|to |</V>
<V>|non |strin|ger |ma |ral|lar|ga o|gne |vi|go|re |</V>
<V>|tu |se’ |o|mai |al |pur|ga|to|rio |giun|to |</V>
<T><V>|ve|di |là il |bal|zo |che ’l |chiu|de |din|tor|no |</V>
<V>|ve|di |l’ en|tra|ta |là |’ve |par |di|giun|to |</V>
<V>|dian|zi |ne |l’ al|ba |che |pro|ce|de al |gior|no |</V>
<T><V>|so|vra |li |fio|ri on|d’ è |là |giù |ad|dor|no |</V>
<V>|la|scia|te|mi |pi|gliar |co|stui |che |dor|me |</V>
<V>|sor|del |ri|ma|se e |l’ al|tre |gen|ti |for|me |</V>
<T><V>|el|la |ti |tol|se e |co|me ’l |dì |fu |chia|ro |</V>

<V>|qui |ti |po|sò |ma |pria |mi |di|mo|stra|ro |</V>
<T><V>|li oc|chi |suoi |bel|li |quel|la in|tra|ta a|per|ta |</V>

<T><V>|per |gi|re ad |es|sa |di |co|lor |di|ver|si |</V>

<V>|ve|ni|te |dun|que a’ |no|stri |gra|di in|nan|zi |</V>

<V>|por|fi|do |mi |pa|rea |sì |fiam|meg|gian|te |</V>

<V>|so|vra |sen|na|che|rìb |den|tro |dal |tem|pio |</V>
<V>|e |co|me |mor|to |lui |qui|vi il |la|scia|ro |</V>
<T><V>|mo|stra|va |la |ru|i|na e ’l |cru|do |scem|pio |</V>

<V>|san|gue |si|ti|sti e |io |di |san|gue |t’ em|pio |</V>

<V>|di |sov|r’ es|so |re|ch’ io |que|sta |per|so|na |</V>
<T><V>|dir|vi |ch’ i’ |sia |sa|ria |par|la|re in|dar|no |</V>
<V>|ché ’l |no|me |mio |an|cor |mol|to |non |suo|na |</V>
<V>|se |ben |lo ’n|ten|di|men|to |tuo |ac|car|no |</V>
<T><V>|con |lo ’n|tel|let|to al|lo|ra |mi |ri|spuo|se |</V>
<V>|quei |che |di|ce|va |pria |tu |par|li |d’ ar|no |</V>
<V>|e |l’ al|tro |dis|se |lui |per|ché |na|sco|se |</V>
<T><V>|que|sti il |vo|ca|bol |di |quel|la |ri|vie|ra |</V>
<V>|pur |com’ |om |fa |de |l’ or|ri|bi|li |co|se |</V>
<V>|e |l’ om|bra |che |di |ciò |do|man|da|ta e|ra |</V>
<T><V>|si |sde|bi|tò |co|sì |non |so |ma |de|gno |</V>
<V>|ben |è |che ’l |no|me |di |tal |val|le |pè|ra |</V>
<V>|ché |dal |prin|ci|pio |suo |o|v’ è |sì |pre|gno |</V>
<T><V>|l’ al|pe|stro |mon|te on|d’ è |tron|co |pe|lo|ro |</V>
<V>|che ’n |po|chi |luo|ghi |pas|sa ol|tra |quel |se|gno |</V>
<V>|in|fin |là |’ve |si |ren|de |per |ri|sto|ro |</V>
<T><V>|di |quel |che ’l |ciel |de |la |ma|ri|na a|sciu|ga |</V>
<V>|on|d’ han|no i |fiu|mi |ciò |che |va |con |lo|ro |</V>
<V>|ver|tù |co|sì |per |ni|mi|ca |si |fu|ga |</V>
<T><V>|da |tut|ti |co|me |bi|scia o |per |sven|tu|ra |</V>
<V>|del |luo|go o |per |mal |u|so |che |li |fru|ga |</V>
<V>|on|d’ han|no |sì |mu|ta|ta |lor |na|tu|ra |</V>
<T><V>|li a|bi|ta|tor |de |la |mi|se|ra |val|le |</V>
<V>|che |par |che |cir|ce |li a|ves|se in |pa|stu|ra |</V>
<V>|tra |brut|ti |por|ci |più |de|gni |di |gal|le |</V>
<T><V>|che |d’ al|tro |ci|bo |fat|to in |u|man |u|so |</V>
<V>|di|riz|za |pri|ma il |suo |po|ve|ro |cal|le |</V>
<V>|bo|to|li |tro|va |poi |ve|nen|do |giu|so |</V>
<T><V>|rin|ghio|si |più |che |non |chie|de |lor |pos|sa |</V>

<V>|vas|si |cag|gen|do e |quan|t’ el|la |più ’n|gros|sa |</V>
<T><V>|tan|to |più |tro|va |di |can |far|si |lu|pi |</V>

<V>|di|sce|sa |poi |per |più |pe|la|ghi |cu|pi |</V>
<T><V>|tro|va |le |vol|pi |sì |pie|ne |di |fro|da |</V>

<V>|né |la|sce|rò |di |dir |per|ch’ al|tri |m’ o|da |</V>
<T><V>|e |buon |sa|rà |co|stui |s’ an|cor |s’ am|men|ta |</V>
<V>|di |ciò |che |ve|ro |spir|to |mi |di|sno|da |</V>
<V>|io |veg|gio |tuo |ne|po|te |che |di|ven|ta |</V>
<T><V>|cac|cia|tor |di |quei |lu|pi in |su |la |ri|va |</V>

<V>|ven|de |la |car|ne |lo|ro es|sen|do |vi|va |</V>
<T><V>|po|scia |li an|ci|de |co|me an|ti|ca |bel|va |</V>

<V>|san|gui|no|so e|sce |de |la |tri|sta |sel|va |</V>

<V>|tan|to |sua |gra|zia |non |ti |sa|rò |scar|so |</V>

<T><V>|là |’v’ è |me|stier |di |con|sor|te |di|vie|to |</V>

<V>|de |la |ca|sa |da |cal|bo|li o|ve |nul|lo |</V>
<T><V>|fat|to |s’ è |re|da |poi |del |suo |va|lo|re |</V>

<V>|del |ben |ri|che|sto al |ve|ro e |al |tra|stul|lo |</V>
<T><V>|ché |den|tro a |que|sti |ter|mi|ni è |ri|pie|no |</V>

<V>|per |col|ti|va|re o|mai |ver|reb|ber |me|no |</V>
<T><V>|o|v’ è ’l |buon |li|zio e |ar|ri|go |mai|nar|di |</V>
<V>|pier |tra|ver|sa|ro e |gui|do |di |car|pi|gna |</V>
<V>|oh |ro|ma|gnuo|li |tor|na|ti in |ba|star|di |</V>
<T><V>|quan|do in |bo|lo|gna un |fab|bro |si |ral|li|gna |</V>

<V>|ver|ga |gen|til |di |pic|cio|la |gra|mi|gna |</V>
<T><V>|non |ti |ma|ra|vi|gliar |s’ io |pian|go |to|sco |</V>

<V>|con |quel|lo a|spet|to |che |pie|tà |di|ser|ra |</V>
<T><V>|quan|do |l’ a|ni|ma |mia |tor|nò |di |fo|ri |</V>
<V>|a |le |co|se |che |son |fuor |di |lei |ve|re |</V>
<V>|io |ri|co|nob|bi i |miei |non |fal|si er|ro|ri |</V>
<T><V>|lo |du|ca |mio |che |mi |po|tea |ve|de|re |</V>
<V>|far |sì |com’ |om |che |dal |son|no |si |sle|ga |</V>
<V>|dis|se |che |hai |che |non |ti |puoi |te|ne|re |</V>
<T><V>|ma |se’ |ve|nu|to |più |che |mez|za |le|ga |</V>

<V>|a |gui|sa |di |cui |vi|no o |son|no |pie|ga |</V>
<T><V>|o |dol|ce |pa|dre |mio |se |tu |m’ a|scol|te |</V>

<T><V>|ve|de|sti |dis|se |quel|l’ an|ti|ca |stre|ga |</V>
<V>|che |so|la |sov|r’ a |noi |o|mai |si |pia|gne |</V>
<V>|ve|de|sti |co|me |l’ uom |da |lei |si |sle|ga |</V>
<T><V>|ba|sti|ti e |bat|ti a |ter|ra |le |cal|ca|gne |</V>
<V>|li oc|chi |ri|vol|gi al |lo|go|ro |che |gi|ra |</V>
<V>|lo |re|ge et|ter|no |con |le |ro|te |ma|gne |</V>
<T><V>|qua|le ’l |fal|con |che |pri|ma a’ |pié |si |mi|ra |</V>

<V>|per |lo |di|sio |del |pa|sto |che |là il |ti|ra |</V>

<V>|se |voi |sie|te om|bre |che |dio |sù |non |de|gni |</V>
<V>|chi |v’ ha |per |la |sua |sca|la |tan|to |scor|te |</V>
<T><V>|e ’l |dot|tor |mio |se |tu |ri|guar|di a’ |se|gni |</V>

<V>|ben |ve|drai |che |coi |buon |con|vien |ch’ e’ |re|gni |</V>
<T><V>|ma |per|ché |lei |che |dì |e |not|te |fi|la |</V>
<V>|non |li a|vea |trat|ta an|co|ra |la |co|noc|chia |</V>
<V>|che |clo|to im|po|ne a |cia|scu|no e |com|pi|la |</V>
<T><V>|l’ a|ni|ma |sua |ch’ è |tua |e |mia |se|roc|chia |</V>

<V>|pe|rò |ch’ al |no|stro |mo|do |non |a|doc|chia |</V>

<T><V>|per |es|ser |pur |al|lo|ra |vòl|to in |la|ci |</V>
<V>|vi|di |gen|te |sot|t’ es|so al|zar |le |ma|ni |</V>
<V>|e |gri|dar |non |so |che |ver|so |le |fron|de |</V>
<T><V>|qua|si |bra|mo|si |fan|to|li|ni e |va|ni |</V>
<V>|che |pre|ga|no e ’l |pre|ga|to |non |ri|spon|de |</V>
<V>|ma |per |fa|re es|ser |ben |la |vo|glia a|cu|ta |</V>
<T><V>|poi |si |par|tì |sì |co|me |ri|cre|du|ta |</V>

<V>|e |que|sta |pian|ta |si |le|vò |da |es|so |</V>
<T><V>|sì |tra |le |fra|sche |non |so |chi |di|ce|va |</V>

<V>|mo|stra|va |l’ al|tro |la |con|tra|ria |cu|ra |</V>

<V>|poi |vi|di |quat|tro in |u|mi|le |pa|ru|ta |</V>

<V>|per |che |di|ven|ne |mo|stro e |po|scia |pre|da |</V>
<T><V>|ch’ io |veg|gio |cer|ta|men|te e |pe|rò il |nar|ro |</V>
<V>|a |dar|ne |tem|po |già |stel|le |pro|pin|que |</V>
<V>|se|cu|re |d’ og|n’ in|top|po e |d’ o|gne |sbar|ro |</V>
<T><V>|nel |qua|le un |cin|que|cen|to |die|ce e |cin|que |</V>
<V>|con |quel |gi|gan|te |che |con |lei |de|lin|que |</V>
<V>|e |for|se |che |la |mia |nar|ra|zion |bu|ia |</V>
<T><V>|qual |te|mi e |sfin|ge |men |ti |per|su|a|de |</V>

<V>|ma |to|sto |fier |li |fat|ti |le |na|ia|de |</V>

<V>|da |la |mia |de|stra |par|te e |che |s’ ac|cen|de |</V>
<T><V>|di |tut|to il |lu|me |de |la |spe|ra |no|stra |</V>
<V>|ciò |ch’ io |di|co |di |me |di |sé |in|ten|de |</V>
<V>|so|rel|la |fu |e |co|sì |le |fu |tol|ta |</V>
<T><V>|di |ca|po |l’ om|bra |de |le |sa|cre |ben|de |</V>

<T><V>|non |fu |dal |vel |del |cor |già |mai |di|sciol|ta |</V>

<T><V>|ge|ne|rò ’l |ter|zo e |l’ ul|ti|ma |pos|san|za |</V>

<V>|co|me |fo|co |di |nu|be |si |di|ser|ra |</V>
<V>|per |di|la|tar|si |sì |che |non |vi |ca|pe |</V>
<T><V>|e |fuor |di |sua |na|tu|ra in |giù |s’ at|ter|ra |</V>
<V>|la |men|te |mia |co|sì |tra |quel|le |da|pe |</V>
<V>|e |che |si |fes|se |ri|mem|brar |non |sa|pe |</V>
<T><V>|tu |hai |ve|du|te |co|se |che |pos|sen|te |</V>
<V>|di |vi|sï|o|ne o|bli|ta e |che |s’ in|ge|gna |</V>
<V>|in|dar|no |di |ri|dur|la|si a |la |men|te |</V>
<T><V>|quan|d’ io |u|di’ |que|sta |pro|fer|ta |de|gna |</V>
<V>|di |tan|to |gra|to |che |mai |non |si |stin|gue |</V>
<V>|del |li|bro |che ’l |pre|te|ri|to |ras|se|gna |</V>
<T><V>|se |mo |so|nas|ser |tut|te |quel|le |lin|gue |</V>
<V>|che |po|lim|nï|a |con |le |suo|re |fe|ro |</V>
<V>|del |lat|te |lor |dol|cis|si|mo |più |pin|gue |</V>
<T><V>|per |a|iu|tar|mi al |mil|le|smo |del |ve|ro |</V>
<V>|non |si |ver|ria |can|tan|do il |san|to |ri|so |</V>
<V>|e |quan|to il |san|to a|spet|to |fa|cea |me|ro |</V>
<T><V>|e |co|sì |fi|gu|ran|do il |pa|ra|di|so |</V>

<V>|co|me |chi |tro|va |suo |cam|min |ri|ci|so |</V>
<T><V>|ma |chi |pen|sas|se il |pon|de|ro|so |te|ma |</V>

<V>|nol |bia|sme|reb|be |se |sot|t’ es|so |tre|ma |</V>
<T><V>|non |è |pa|reg|gio |da |pic|cio|la |bar|ca |</V>

<T><V>|per|ché |la |fac|cia |mia |sì |t’ in|na|mo|ra |</V>

<V>|che |sot|to i |rag|gi |di |cri|sto |s’ in|fio|ra |</V>
<T><V>|qui|vi è |la |ro|sa in |che ’l |ver|bo |di|vi|no |</V>

<V>|al |cui |o|dor |si |pre|se il |buon |cam|mi|no |</V>

<V>|di |dio |e |di |ma|ria |di |sua |vit|to|ria |</V>

<V>|tal |e|ra |io |a |quel|la |vi|sta |no|va |</V>
<V>|ve|der |vo|le|va |co|me |si |con|ven|ne |</V>
<T><V>|l’ i|ma|go al |cer|chio e |co|me |vi |s’ in|do|va |</V>
<V>|ma |non |e|ran |da |ciò |le |pro|prie |pen|ne |</V>
<V>|se |non |che |la |mia |men|te |fu |per|cos|sa |</V>
<T><V>|da |un |ful|go|re in |che |sua |vo|glia |ven|ne |</V>
<V>|a |l’ al|ta |fan|ta|sia |qui |man|cò |pos|sa |</V>
<V>|sì |co|me |ro|ta |ch’ i|gual|men|te è |mos|sa |</V>
<T><V>|l’ a|mor |che |mo|ve il |so|le e |l’ al|tre |stel|le |</V>
